(** * Bicategory of Display Map Categories
    NOTE: The displayed version of this category should be used instead of this.
          Everything in this file is mirrored in that version.

    This file contains a direct construction of the bicategory of display map categories with a terminal object in their base category.
    It adds the terminal condition to make the construction of the pseudofunctor possible.

    Contents:
    - bicategory of display map categories [bicat_display_map_cat]
    - pseudofunctor into the bicategory of full comprehension categories [bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat]
 *)

UU
?ob → ?ob → UU
∏ X Y : ?ob, ?mor X Y → ?mor X Y → UU
∏ X : ?ob, ?mor X X
∏ X Y Z : ?ob, ?mor X Y → ?mor Y Z → ?mor X Z
∏ (X Y : ?ob) (f : ?mor X Y), ?cell X Y f f
∏ (X Y : ?ob) (f g h : ?mor X Y),
?cell X Y f g → ?cell X Y g h → ?cell X Y f h
∏ (X Y Z : ?ob) (f : ?mor X Y) (g h : ?mor Y Z),
?cell Y Z g h
→ ?cell X Z (?comp X Y Z f g) (?comp X Y Z f h)
∏ (X Y Z : ?ob) (g h : ?mor X Y) (f : ?mor Y Z),
?cell X Y g h
→ ?cell X Z (?comp X Y Z g f) (?comp X Y Z h f)
∏ (X Y : ?ob) (f : ?mor X Y),
?cell X Y (?comp X X Y (?id₁ X) f) f
∏ (X Y : ?ob) (f : ?mor X Y),
?cell X Y f (?comp X X Y (?id₁ X) f)
∏ (X Y : ?ob) (f : ?mor X Y),
?cell X Y (?comp X Y Y f (?id₁ Y)) f
∏ (X Y : ?ob) (f : ?mor X Y),
?cell X Y f (?comp X Y Y f (?id₁ Y))
∏ (W X Y Z : ?ob) (f : ?mor W X) (g : ?mor X Y)
(h : ?mor Y Z),
?cell W Z (?comp W X Z f (?comp X Y Z g h))
  (?comp W Y Z (?comp W X Y f g) h)
∏ (W X Y Z : ?ob) (f : ?mor W X) (g : ?mor X Y)
(h : ?mor Y Z),
?cell W Z (?comp W Y Z (?comp W X Y f g) h)
  (?comp W X Z f (?comp X Y Z g h))

D₁: display_map_class C₁

(a
 b : ∑ C : univalent_category,
     Terminal C × display_map_class C)
(f g h
 k : ∑
     F : display_map_class_functor (pr22 a) (pr22 b),
     preserves_terminal F) (x : pr1 f ⟹ pr1 g)
(y : pr1 g ⟹ pr1 h) (z : pr1 h ⟹ pr1 k),
nat_trans_comp (pr1 f) (pr1 g) (pr1 k) x
  (nat_trans_comp (pr1 g) (pr1 h) (pr1 k) y z) =

C₁: univalent_category
TC₁: Terminal C₁
D₁: display_map_class C₁
C₂: univalent_category
TC₂: Terminal C₂
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
pT_F: preserves_terminal F
G: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
pT_G: preserves_terminal G
H: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
pT_H: preserves_terminal H
I: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
pT_I: preserves_terminal I
α: F ⟹ G
β: G ⟹ H
γ: H ⟹ I
nat_trans_comp F G I α (nat_trans_comp G H I β γ) =
nat_trans_comp F H I (nat_trans_comp F G H α β) γ

    exact (nat_trans_comp_assoc (pr21 C₂) _ _ _ _ _ _ _).

(a b

∏
(a b c
 d : ∑ C : univalent_category,
     Terminal C × display_map_class C)
(f : ∑
     F : display_map_class_functor (pr22 a) (pr22 b),
     preserves_terminal F)
(g
 h : ∑
     F : display_map_class_functor (pr22 b) (pr22 c),
     preserves_terminal F)
(i : ∑
     F : display_map_class_functor (pr22 c) (pr22 d),
     preserves_terminal F) (x : pr1 g ⟹ pr1 h),
nat_trans_comp
  (functor_composite_data (pr11 f)
     (functor_composite_data (pr11 g) (pr11 i)))
  (functor_composite_data (pr11 f)
     (functor_composite_data (pr11 h) (pr11 i)))

  (functor_composite_data
     (functor_identity_data (pr1 a)) (pr11 f))

(** Some functions for clarity *)
Definition display_map_univ_cat : UU := bicat_display_map_cat.

bicat_display_map_cat_ob_to_display_map_univ_cat does
not respect the uniform inheritance condition.
[uniform-inheritance,coercions,default]


Coercion display_map_cat_to_base_category (D : display_map_univ_cat) : univalent_category := pr1 D.


New coercion path [display_map_cat_to_terminal_category;
                   TerminalObject;
                   bicat_display_map_cat_ob_to_display_map_univ_cat] : display_map_univ_cat >-> display_map_univ_cat is not definitionally an identity function.
New coercion path [bicat_display_map_cat_ob_to_display_map_univ_cat;
                   display_map_cat_to_terminal_category;
                   TerminalObject] : ob >-> ob is not definitionally an identity function.
New coercion path [TerminalObject;
                   bicat_display_map_cat_ob_to_display_map_univ_cat;
                   display_map_cat_to_terminal_category] : Terminal >-> Terminal is not definitionally an identity function.
[ambiguous-paths,coercions,default]


Coercion display_map_cat_to_display_map_class (D : display_map_univ_cat) : display_map_class (display_map_cat_to_base_category D) := pr22 D.

Definition display_map_cat_functor (D₁ D₂ : bicat_display_map_cat) : UU := bicat_display_map_cat ⟦D₁, D₂⟧.

bicat_display_map_mor_to_display_map_cat_functor does
not respect the uniform inheritance condition.
[uniform-inheritance,coercions,default]


Coercion display_map_functor_to_display_map_class_functor {D₁ D₂ : bicat_display_map_cat} (F : display_map_cat_functor D₁ D₂) : display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂ := pr1 F.

Coercion display_map_functor_preserves_terminal {D₁ D₂ : bicat_display_map_cat} (F : display_map_cat_functor D₁ D₂) : preserves_terminal F := pr2 F.

                                  (disp_cat_of_types x))),

                is_full_comp_cat x) (x0 : pr1 x)

              (Fibrations.disp_functor_of_cartesian_disp_functor
                 (pr21 x) x0 xx)))
        (λ (x : ∑

∏ (D₁ D₂ D₃ : bicat_display_map_cat)
(F : bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧)
(G : bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧),
display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₂ F
· display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₂ D₃ G ==>
display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₃ (F · G)

  
∏ (D₁ D₂ D₃ : bicat_display_map_cat)
(F : bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧)
(G : bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧),
display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₂ F
· display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₂ D₃ G ==>
display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₃ (F · G)

F: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
G: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₂ F
· display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₂ D₃ G ==>
display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₃ (F · G)
 
D₁, D₂, D₃: bicat_display_map_cat
F: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
G: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
comp_cat_nat_trans
  (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₂ F
   · display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₂ D₃ G)
  (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₃
     (F · G))

  (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₃
     (F · G))

G: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
comprehension_nat_trans_eq ?τ
  (comp_cat_functor_comprehension
     (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₂ F
      · display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₂ D₃
          G))
  (comp_cat_functor_comprehension
     (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₃
        (F · G)))

    
D₁, D₂, D₃: bicat_display_map_cat
F: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
G: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
nat_trans_with_terminal_cleaving
  (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₂ F
   · display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₂ D₃ G)
  (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₃
     (F · G))
 
D₁, D₂, D₃: bicat_display_map_cat
F: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
G: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
nat_trans_with_terminal_disp_cat
  (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₂ F
   · display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₂ D₃ G)
  (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₃
     (F · G))
 
D₁, D₂, D₃: bicat_display_map_cat
F: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
G: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
(display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₂ F
 · display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₂ D₃ G)
⟹ display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₃
    (F · G)
D₁, D₂, D₃: bicat_display_map_cat

G: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
disp_nat_trans ?τ
  (comp_cat_type_functor
     (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₂ F
      · display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₂ D₃
          G))
  (comp_cat_type_functor
     (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₃
        (F · G)))

      
D₁, D₂, D₃: bicat_display_map_cat
F: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
G: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
(display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₂ F
 · display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₂ D₃ G)
⟹ display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₃
    (F · G)
 exact (nat_trans_id _).
      
D₁, D₂, D₃: bicat_display_map_cat
F: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
G: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧

  (nat_trans_id
     (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₂ F
      · display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₂ D₃
          G))
  (comp_cat_type_functor
     (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₂ F
      · display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₂ D₃
          G))
  (comp_cat_type_functor
     (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₃
        (F · G)))
 exact display_map_functor_composite_to_composite_display_map_functor.
    
D₁, D₂, D₃: bicat_display_map_cat
F: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
G: bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
comprehension_nat_trans_eq
  (make_nat_trans_with_terminal_cleaving
     (make_nat_trans_with_terminal_disp_cat
        (nat_trans_id
           (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁
              D₂ F
            · display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor
                D₂ D₃ G))
        display_map_functor_composite_to_composite_display_map_functor))
  (comp_cat_functor_comprehension
     (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₂ F
      · display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₂ D₃
          G))
  (comp_cat_functor_comprehension
     (display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor D₁ D₃
        (F · G)))
 abstract (intros x dx; cbn; rewrite ? (pr12 (pr11 G)); exact (!assoc _ _ _ @ id_left _ @ id_left _ @ !id_right _)).
  Defined.

  
psfunctor_data bicat_display_map_cat
  bicat_full_comp_cat

  
psfunctor_data bicat_display_map_cat
  bicat_full_comp_cat

    
bicat_display_map_cat → bicat_full_comp_cat
∏ a b : bicat_display_map_cat,
bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ a, b ⟧
→ bicat_full_comp_cat ⟦ ?F₀ a, ?F₀ b ⟧
∏ (a b : bicat_display_map_cat)
(f g : bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ a, b ⟧),
f ==> g → ?F₁ a b f ==> ?F₁ a b g
∏ a : bicat_display_map_cat,
id₁ (?F₀ a) ==> ?F₁ a a (id₁ a)
∏ (a b c : bicat_display_map_cat)
(f : bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ a, b ⟧)
(g : bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ b, c ⟧),
?F₁ a b f · ?F₁ b c g ==> ?F₁ a c (f · g)

    
bicat_display_map_cat → bicat_full_comp_cat
 exact display_map_cat_to_full_comp_cat.
    
∏ a b : bicat_display_map_cat,
bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ a, b ⟧
→ bicat_full_comp_cat
  ⟦ display_map_cat_to_full_comp_cat a,
  display_map_cat_to_full_comp_cat b ⟧
 exact display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor.
    
∏ (a b : bicat_display_map_cat)
(f g : bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ a, b ⟧),
f ==> g
→ display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor a b f ==>
  display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor a b g
 exact display_map_transformation_to_comp_cat_transformation.
    
∏ a : bicat_display_map_cat,
id₁ (display_map_cat_to_full_comp_cat a) ==>
display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor a a (id₁ a)
 exact display_map_to_comp_cat_id_1cell.
    
∏ (a b c : bicat_display_map_cat)
(f : bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ a, b ⟧)
(g : bicat_display_map_cat ⟦ b, c ⟧),
display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor a b f
· display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor b c g ==>
display_map_functor_to_comp_cat_functor a c (f · g)
 exact display_map_to_comp_cat_comp_1cell.
  Defined.

      C₁ TC₁ D₁ C₂ TC₂ D₂ C₃ TC₃ D₃ F G x dx)
   :

 abstract (intros x₁ x₂ f dx₁ dx₂ [df Hsq];

  Defined.

     (# bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_data
        (F · G)))
  (make_full_comp_cat_nat_trans
     (make_comp_cat_nat_trans
        (make_nat_trans_with_terminal_cleaving
           (make_nat_trans_with_terminal_disp_cat
              (nat_trans_id
                 (# bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_data
                    (F · G)))
              (bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_comp_2cell
                 (C₁,, TC₁,, D₁) (C₂,, TC₂,, D₂)
                 (C₃,, TC₃,, D₃) F G)))
        ((λ (x : bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_data
                   (C₁,, TC₁,, D₁))
          (dx : Univalence.disp_cat_of_disp_univalent_cat
                  (disp_cat_of_types
                     (bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_data
                        (C₁,, TC₁,, D₁))) x),
          internal_paths_rew_r
            (C₃ ⟦ G (F (pr1 dx)), G (F (pr1 dx)) ⟧)
            (# G (id₁ (F (pr1 dx))))
            (id₁ (G (F (pr1 dx))))
            (λ p : C₃ ⟦ G (F (pr1 dx)), G (F (pr1 dx))
                   ⟧,
             id₁ ((pr11 G) ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx)))
             · id₁ ((pr11 G) ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx))) =
             id₁ ((pr11 G) ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx)))
             · (p · id₁ (G (F (pr1 dx)))))
            (internal_paths_rew_r
               (C₃ ⟦ (pr11 G) ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx)),
                G (F (pr1 dx)) ⟧)
               (id₁ ((pr11 G) ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx)))
                · id₁ ((pr11 G) ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx))))
               (id₁ ((pr11 G) ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx))))
               (λ p : C₃
                      ⟦ (pr11 G) ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx)),
                      G (F (pr1 dx)) ⟧,
                p =
                id₁ ((pr11 G) ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx)))
                · (id₁ (G (F (pr1 dx)))
                   · id₁ (G (F (pr1 dx)))))
               (internal_paths_rew_r
                  (C₃ ⟦ (pr11 G) ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx)),
                   G (F (pr1 dx)) ⟧)
                  (id₁ ((pr11 G) ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx)))
                   · (id₁ (G (F (pr1 dx)))
                      · id₁ (G (F (pr1 dx)))))
                  (id₁ (G (F (pr1 dx)))
                   · id₁ (G (F (pr1 dx))))
                  (λ p : C₃
                         ⟦ (pr11 G)
                             ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx)),
                         G (F (pr1 dx)) ⟧,
                   id₁ ((pr11 G) ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx))) =
                   p)
                  (internal_paths_rew_r
                     (C₃ ⟦ G (F (pr1 dx)),
                      G (F (pr1 dx)) ⟧)
                     (id₁ (G (F (pr1 dx)))
                      · id₁ (G (F (pr1 dx))))
                     (id₁ (G (F (pr1 dx))))
                     (λ p : C₃ ⟦ G (F (pr1 dx)),
                            G (F (pr1 dx)) ⟧,
                      id₁
                        ((pr11 G) ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx))) =
                      p)
                     (idpath
                        (id₁
                           ((pr11 G)
                              ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx)))))
                     (id_left (id₁ (G (F (pr1 dx))))))
                  (id_left
                     (id₁ (G (F (pr1 dx)))
                      · id₁ (G (F (pr1 dx))))))
               (id_left
                  (id₁ ((pr11 G) ((pr11 F) (pr1 dx))))))
            (functor_id G (F (pr1 dx)))
          :
          comprehension_nat_trans_mor
            (comp_cat_functor_comprehension
               (# bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_data
                  (F · G))) dx
          · comprehension_functor_mor
              (comp_cat_comprehension
                 (bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_data
                    (C₃,, TC₃,, D₃)))
              (comp_cat_type_nat_trans
                 (make_nat_trans_with_terminal_cleaving
                    (make_nat_trans_with_terminal_disp_cat
                       (nat_trans_id
                          (# bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_data
                             (F · G)))
                       (bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_comp_2cell
                          (C₁,, TC₁,, D₁)
                          (C₂,, TC₂,, D₂)
                          (C₃,, TC₃,, D₃) F G))) x dx) =
          make_nat_trans_with_terminal_cleaving
            (make_nat_trans_with_terminal_disp_cat
               (nat_trans_id
                  (# bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_data
                     (F · G)))
               (bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_comp_2cell
                  (C₁,, TC₁,, D₁) (C₂,, TC₂,, D₂)
                  (C₃,, TC₃,, D₃) F G))
            (comprehension_functor_ob
               (comp_cat_comprehension
                  (bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_data
                     (C₁,, TC₁,, D₁))) dx)
          · comprehension_nat_trans_mor
              (comp_cat_functor_comprehension
                 (# bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_data
                    F
                  · # bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_data
                      G)) dx)
         :
         comprehension_nat_trans_eq
           (make_nat_trans_with_terminal_cleaving
              (make_nat_trans_with_terminal_disp_cat
                 (nat_trans_id
                    (# bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_data
                       (F · G)))
                 (bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_comp_2cell
                    (C₁,, TC₁,, D₁) (C₂,, TC₂,, D₂)
                    (C₃,, TC₃,, D₃) F G)))
           (comp_cat_functor_comprehension
              (# bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_data
                 (F · G)))
           (comp_cat_functor_comprehension
              (# bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_data
                 F
               · # bicat_display_map_cat_to_bicat_full_comp_cat_data
                   G)))))
 split; use full_comp_nat_trans_eq;
      [ intros x; exact (id_left _)
      | intros x dx; use subtypePath; try (exact (λ _, homset_property _ _ _ _ _)); etrans;
        [ refine (pr1_transportf (A := C₃⟦_, _⟧) _ _ @ _); rewrite transportf_const;
          apply id_left | exact (idpath _) ]
      | intros x; exact (id_left _)
      | intros x dx; use subtypePath; try (exact (λ _, homset_property _ _ _ _ _)); etrans;
        [ refine (pr1_transportf (A := C₃⟦_, _⟧) _ _ @ _); rewrite transportf_const;
          apply id_left | exact (idpath _) ]].
  Qed.
